Digital Delta Eco Extensions - Discovery API documentation version 0.9

https://ddecotest.aquadesk.nl

About

The Digital Delta Eco API is a specialization of the original Digital Delta API. The Eco API is focused on measurements in the Ecology realm (taxa, chemicals, physical objects), where measurements are mostly observation-based, instead of being measured by automated systems.

Due to this, the measurements are not on a fixed time schedule. Therefore, the time series are less usable for the Eco API.

Another reason for a specialization is that the data is less uniform: one sample can contain multiple organisms or chemicals. Furthermore, additional meta-data might be specified with measurements.

A list of implementations of the API is available here.

The current specification version is 0.9 with status 'Proposal'.

Ecological Measurements

Ecological measurements are divers, and mostly not a goal, but a means. A means to produce a spreadsheet, display a map, analyse what happens to a species in time, analyse the quality of a body of water, required reporting to the government, etc.

To be able to provide relevant information, the following is stored with a measurement:

TopicDescription
WhoWhat organisation requested the measurement and/or performed the sampling/analysis.
WhenWhen the sample was taken, the analysis performed. Ecological measurements are mostly non-automated and non-continuous.
WhereWhere the measurement was taken. This includes a position, but also what compartment such as open water, shore, vegetation. Some measurements are taken on a boat, so the position of the measurement may not be fixed and can differ from the location where the measurement object.
WhatThis can range from a single chemical, to multiple kinds of species per measurement. Next to the parameter (mostly applies to species), more specifications might be requested, such as life stage, gender, behaviour.
WhyThe reason why the measurement took place. Was it, for instance, for a regular monitoring, was it for a specific project, was it for assessments, etc.
HowThe how described how a sample was taken, for instance: what fish net was used, what size the holes in the net were, what handbook was used to sample, or to analyse, etc.

To allow those questions to be answered, the information required to answer those questions, need to be stored. That makes ecological measurements more complex, since that meta-information varies.

Furthermore, many ecological measurements require manual labour (getting the sample, preparing the sample, observing the sample) and are not measured in a fixed interval. Time series are therefore a much less useful format for this type of measurements.

Measurement level

The Measurement level API is required and is filterable and pageable. An optional geojson specifier is recommended. The expandable specifier is optional. The RAML definition is here.

Discovery level

The Discovery level is build op top of the Measurement level. All end-points in this API are optional, except for the /Endpoints end-point. These end-points are used to discover the possible values and codes that the provider has available for querying measurements.

The RAML definition is here.

Implementation topics

Filter Syntax

Filtering can be performed by constructing a search filter using the following syntax:

<parametername>:<comparer>:<comparevalue>[;<parametername>:<comparer>:<comparevalue>]

ComparerDescriptionData types
eqequalstring, date, number
neunequalstring, date, number
ltless thandate, number
leless than or equal todate, number
gegreater than or equal todate, number
gtgreater thandate, number
initem is one of the values in the liststring, number
notitem is NOT one of the values in the liststring, number
likeString contains the value.string
startswithString starts with the value.string
endswithString ends with the value.string
inbboxItem is within the bounding box, defined by 4 numbersbbox
inpolygonItem is within the polygon, defined by list of numbers, where each x and y are a numbers in the arraybbox
notinbboxItem is NOT within the bounding box, defined by 4 numberspolygon
notinpolygonItem is NOT within the polygon, defined by list of numbers, where each x and y are a numbers in the arraypolygon
wktItem is within the Well-known-text definitionWkt
allall items in the list must be present in the queried itemstring, number
Formatting
String compares are NOT case sensitive and must be surrounded by quotes.
Arrays are expressed in JSON format. This means that they are surrounded by square brackets ([ and ]) and the array values are separated by comma's.
Parameter names are NOT case sensitive.
Number formats are in US notation. This means fractional separators are periods. Comma's (thousands-separators) are ignored.
Date field notation is yyyy-MM-dd and must be surrounded by quotes.
Bbox type requires an array of 4 numeric values. The uneven-numbers represent an X-ordinate, the even-numbers represent an Y-ordinates. The uneven and the following even number represent a coordinate in WGS84.
Polygon type requires an array of numeric values. The number of items in the array need to be even. The uneven-numbers represent an X-ordinate, the even-numbers represent an Y-ordinates. The uneven and the following even number represent a coordinate in WGS84.
Examples
location:eq:"NLKAD";parameter:eq:"Eukariota";organisation:eq:"RWS",measuredvalue:gt:1000;measuredunitSymbol:eq:"n"
location:in:["NKLAD","NKLBVA","NLKBRA"];parameter:eq:"Eukariota";organisation:eq:"RWS";measuredvalue:gt:1000,measuredunitSymbol:eq:"n"
location:in:["NKLAD","NKLBVA","NLKBRA"];parameter:in:["Eukariota [1]","Plantae"];measuredvalue:gt:1000;measuredunitSymbol:eq:"n"
locationArea:inpolygon:[1,2,3,4];parameterCode:in:["Eukariota [1]","Plantae"];measuredvalue:gt:1000;

Example of a filter in a URL: /organisations/?filter=organisation:eq:"RWS"

Sorting is the responsibility of the caller. It is the responsibility of the provider to always return results in the same order.

General URL syntax: available parameters on the root level:

FieldMeaning
filterSee 'FilterSyntax'.
pageReturns the specified page of records. See 'Paging logic'.
pagesizeThe maximum number of records returned for the page. See 'Paging logic'.

Error Handling

When errors are encountered, error information is provided as follows: The HTTP status code is set to be a value between 400 and 499. The response body has the structure of the Problem type (see 'Minimal'):

{
  "type": "Filter query syntax",
  "title": "Query syntax",
  "typeinfo": null,
  "status": 400,
  "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
  "Ã¬nstance": null,
  "errors": [
      {
          "errortype": "InvalidValue",
          "context": "symbol:eq:"
      }
  ]
}

The value of field 'type' contains an error message. The value of field 'typeinfo' is optional and can contain a link to a page explaining the message. The value of field 'title' contains the title of the message. The value of field 'status' has contains the HTTP status code. The value of field 'detail' can provide extra information, such as given in the example. The value of field 'instance' is optional and can contain information that identifies the error and request at the provider. The field 'errors' is optional and can contain further information concerning the error. In the example, it explains what is wrong with the query syntax.

Paging logic

Initialisation

The minimum page> is 1. The provider specifies minimum, maximum and default pagesize>. If pagesize> is not specified, pagesize> is the provider-specified default page size. If page> is not specified, page> is assumed to be 1.

Paging process

  • If <filter> is set, <filter> is applied to the data set.
  • ((<page> - 1) * <pagesize>) records are skipped.
  • A maximum of <pagesize> records are returned from the resulting data set.

To find out what filters are recognised by the service, the /filters segment can be used on the endpoints. The filters segment does not recognise any additional parameters.

Also see 'Error handling' and 'Filter Syntax'.

Contents of the Repository

The structure of this repository is as follows:

DirectoryPurpose
<root>Contains the base RAML definitions, the readme file and the change history.
.NET Filter Syntax ParserContains a sample implementation of a .NET project that parses the Filter Syntax including NUnit tests.
AquaDesk ExamplesJSON responses from AquaDesk for demonstration purposes.
HtmlContains generated HTML documentation in two themes: the slate theme includes types.
LibrariesRAML libraries in use.
PostMan ScriptsContains sample PostMan scripts in PostMan Collection 2.1 format.
SecurityContains Security-related RAML definitions.

/eco

/eco/endpoints get

Retrieves a list of available endpoints.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/endpoints

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Endpoint)

    Items: Endpoint

    • baseuri: required (string)

      Base address of the end-point.

    • description: required (string)

      Description of the end-point.

    • filterable: required (boolean)

      Supports filtering.

    • pageable: required (boolean)

      Supports paging.

    • expandable: required (boolean)

      Supports the /expand specifier.

    • geoJSON: required (boolean)

      Supports the /geojson specifier.

Example:

        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },

        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/compartments get

Retrieves a list of compartments (AQUO).

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/compartments

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Compartment)

    Items: Compartment

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 20,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/compartments?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/compartments?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "CompartmentsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "code": "BS",
            "name": "Bodem / Sediment",
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:32:10.82"
        },
        {
            "code": "LT",
            "name": "Lucht",
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:32:10.82"
        },
        {
            "code": "NT",
            "name": "Niet van toepassing",
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:32:10.82"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/compartments/filters get

get

get /eco/compartments/filters

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: array of object

Items: Filter

  • FieldName: required (string)

/eco/measurementobjects get

Retrieves a list of measurement objects within the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/measurementobjects

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.MeasurementObject)

    Items: MeasurementObject

    • code: required (string)
    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • organisation: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 19960,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/measurementobjects?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/measurementobjects?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "MeasurementObjectsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:05:13.057",
            "code": "AFGDM_0001",
            "description": "NEDHMT",
            "organisation": "RWS"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:05:13.057",
            "code": "AFGDM_0002",
            "description": "VEEN",
            "organisation": "RWS"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:05:13.057",
            "code": "AFGDM_0003",
            "description": "POEDRIJN",
            "organisation": "RWS"
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

get /eco/measurementobjects/geojson

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Response

Query Parameters

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/measurementobjects/expand get

Retrieves an expanded list of measurement objects within the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/measurementobjects/expand

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.ExpandedMeasurementObject)

    Items: ExpandedMeasurementObject

    • code: required (string)
    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • organisation: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)
    • definition: required (array of Extended.Definition)

      Items: Definition

      • standardCode: (union of string or nil)
      • codeinstandard: (union of string or nil)
      • reference: (string)

        Link to the specific item within the standard.

      • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)
    • monitoringnetworks: required (array of string)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 19960,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/measurementobjects/expand?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/measurementobjects/expand?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "ExpandedMeasurementObjectsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "code": "AFGDM_0001",
            "description": "NEDHMT",
            "organisation": "RWS",
            "definition": [],
            "monitoringnetworks": [],
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:34:20.863"
        },
        {
            "code": "AFGDM_0002",
            "description": "VEEN",
            "organisation": "RWS",
            "definition": [],
            "monitoringnetworks": [],
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:34:20.863"
        },
        {
            "code": "AFGDM_0003",
            "description": "POEDRIJN",
            "organisation": "RWS",
            "definition": [],
            "monitoringnetworks": [],
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:34:20.863"
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

/eco/measurementobjects/filters get

get

get /eco/measurementobjects/filters

  • Response

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: array of object

Items: Filter

  • FieldName: required (string)

    Field name.

  • Comparer: required (string)

    Filter comparer.

  • DataType: required (string)

    Filter data type.

Example:

  [
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "eq",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "ne",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "like",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "startswith",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "endswith",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "in",
        "DataType": "ArrayOfStringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "code",
        "Comparer": "notin",
        "DataType": "ArrayOfStringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "eq",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "ne",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "like",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "startswith",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "endswith",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "in",
        "DataType": "ArrayOfStringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "name",
        "Comparer": "notin",
        "DataType": "ArrayOfStringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "attributetype",
        "Comparer": "eq",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "attributetype",
        "Comparer": "ne",
        "DataType": "StringType"
    },
    {
        "FieldName": "attributetype",
        "Comparer": "like",
        "DataType": "StringType"

/eco/organisations get

Retrieves a list of organisations within the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/organisations

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Organisation)

    Items: Organisation

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • numericcode: (number)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 3,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/organisations?page=1&pagesize=1000",
        "prev": null,
        "next": null,
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "OrganisationsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:57.123",
            "code": "RWS",
            "name": "Rijkswaterstaat",
            "numericcode": 80
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:57.123",
            "code": "HHN",
            "name": "HHRS Hollands Noorderkwartier",
            "numericcode": 12
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:57.123",
            "code": "ECS",
            "name": "EcoSys",
            "numericcode": 1000
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/quantities get

Retrieves a list of quantities available in the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/quantities

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Quantity)

    Items: Quantity

    • name: required (string)
    • code: required (string)
    • values: required (array of string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 53,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/quantities?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/quantities?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "QuantitiesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:41:53.26",
            "code": "AANTL",
            "name": "Aantal",
            "values": []
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:41:53.26",
            "code": "AANTPOPVTE",
            "name": "Aantal per oppervlakte",
            "values": []
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:41:53.26",
            "code": "AANTPVLME",
            "name": "Aantal per volume",
            "values": []
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties

/eco/measurementpackages get

Retrieves a list of measurement packages.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/measurementpackages

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.MeasurementPackage)

    Items: MeasurementPackage

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 24,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/measurementpackages?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/measurementpackages?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "MeasurementPackagesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:00:33.477",
            "code": "AF.AB",
            "description": null,
            "name": "AmfibieÃ«n abundantie"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:00:33.477",
            "code": "BG.BD",
            "description": null,
            "name": "Biologische groepen bedekking"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T17:00:33.477",
            "code": "CS.CC",
            "description": null,
            "name": "Chemische stoffen concentraties"
        }
    ]
}

  • pagesize: (integer)

Media type: application/json

  • provider: (object)

/eco/institutes get

Retrieves a list of institutes within the provider's system. An institute defines or manages one or more standards.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/institutes

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Institute)

    Items: Institute

    • code: required (string)

      Code of the institute.

    • name: required (string)

      Name of the institute.

    • reference: (string)

      URL of the institute.

    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 4,
    "links": {
        "self": "?page=1&pagesize=1000",

        "minPageSize": 1
    },

            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",

        },

            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "code": "CAS",

    ]

/eco/monitoringnetworks get

Retrieves a list of monitoring networks (a collection of measurement objects) within the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/monitoringnetworks

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.MonitoringNetwork)

    Items: MonitoringNetwork

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • organisation: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 83,
    "links": {
        "self": "eco/monitoringnetworks?page=3&pagesize=3",
        "prev": "eco/monitoringnetworks?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "next": "eco/monitoringnetworks?page=4&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "MonitoringNetworksListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:22.4",
            "code": "KRW-NL12_120",
            "description": null,
            "name": "NL12_120",
            "organisation": "HHN"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:22.4",
            "code": "KRW-NL12_130",
            "description": null,
            "name": "NL12_130",
            "organisation": "HHN"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:38:22.4",
            "code": "KRW-NL12_140",
            "description": null,
            "name": "NL12-140",
            "organisation": "HHN"
        }
    ]
}

  • Response

    • organisation: required (string)

/eco/parameterpackages get

Retrieves a list of parameter packages available in the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/parameterpackages

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.ParameterPackage)

    Items: ParameterPackage

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)
    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • parameters: (array of string)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 0,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/parameterpackages?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": null,
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "ParameterPackagesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-04-11T14:21:16.67",
            "code": "OEVRPTN",
            "name": "Oeverplanten"
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • description: (union of string or nil)
    • parameters: (array of string)
    • definition: (array of Extended.Definition)

      Items: Definition

      • standardCode: (union of string or nil)
      • codeinstandard: (union of string or nil)
      • reference: (string)

        Link to the specific item within the standard.

      • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)
    • parametertype: (union of string or nil)
    • taxontype: (union of string or nil)
    • parametertypes: (array of string)

    },

        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "ExpandedParameterPackagesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "code": "OEVRPTN",
            "name": "Oeverplanten",
            "parametertype": "Taxon",
            "taxontype": "MACFT",
            "parameters": [
                "Abies procera",
                "Stachys sylvatica",
                "Syringa"
            ],
            "definition": [],
            "changedate": "2018-04-11T14:20:07.173"
        }
    ]

/eco/purposes get

Retrieves a list of (measurement)purposes available in the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/purposes

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Purpose)

    Items: Purpose

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 1,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/purposes?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": null,
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "PurposesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:15:49.51",
            "code": "MT",
            "name": "Monitoring"
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/taxontypes get

Retrieves a list of taxon types available in the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/taxontypes

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.TaxonType)

    Items: TaxonType

    • code: required (string)
    • name: required (string)
    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 14,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/taxontypes?page=1&pagesize=1000",
        "prev": null,
        "next": null,
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "TaxonTypesListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:43:00.243",
            "code": "ZOOPT",
            "name": "Zooplankton"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-07-09T16:43:00.243",

/eco/standards get

Retrieves a list of standards within the provider's system.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/standards

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Extended.Standard)

    Items: Standard

    • institute: required (string)

      Code of the institute.

    • standardcode: required (string)

      code of the instituteCode.

    • reference: (string)

      Link to the standard.

    • standardstype: (string)

      Type of standard

    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 5,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/standards?page=1&pagesize=1000",
        "prev": null,
        "next": null,
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "StandardsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "institute": "ECS",
            "reference": "https://www.ecosys.nl",
            "standardcode": "ECOSYS",
            "standardstype": "Open"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "institute": "ECS",
            "reference": "https://www.aquadesk.nl",
            "standardcode": "AQUADESK",
            "standardstype": "Open"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "institute": "IHW",
            "reference": "https://www.aquo.nl",
            "standardcode": "AQUO",
            "standardstype": "Open"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "institute": "RWS",
            "reference": "http://sofus.ecosys.nl/taxabase.htm",
            "standardcode": "TWN",
            "standardstype": "Open"
        },
        {
            "changedate": "2018-01-01T00:00:00",
            "institute": "ACS",
            "reference": "https://www.cas.org",
            "standardcode": "CAS",
            "standardstype": "Open"
        }
    ]
}

Type: object

/eco/measurements get

Retrieves a list of measurements.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/measurements

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

HTTP status code 200

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • totalObjectCount: required (integer)

    Number of records satisfying the query parameters.

    Example:

    1123
  • links: required (object)

    Default block of links for navigation for all collection pages, except GeoJSON.

    • self: (union of string or nil)

      The URI of the current page.

    • first: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the first page.

    • prev: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the previous page. null if the requested page is the first page.

    • next: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the next page. null if the requested page is the last page.

    • last: (union of string or nil)

      Url to the API holding the last page.

    • maxPageSize: (integer)

      Maximum page size, as defined by the provider.

    • defaultPageSize: required (integer)

      Default page size that the provider uses, if not provided by the consumer.

    • minPageSize: required (integer)

      Minimum page size, as defined by the provider. Cannot be less than 1.

  • result: required (array of Minimal.Measurement)

    Items: Measurement

    • organisation: required (string)

      The code of the organisations that owns the data.

    • measurementobject: required (string)

      The location where the measurements were sampled.

    • locationgeography: (string)

      Coordinates of the measurementobject associated with the measurement if it differentiates from the measurement object.

    • measurementgeography: (string)

      Coordinates of the geographycal position on which the measurement took place.

    • measurementpackage: (union of string or nil)

      The measurement package used for the measurement.

    • measurementpurpose: (union of string or nil)

      The purpose of the measurement.

    • methods: (array of string)

      The methods used for sampling and analysing.

    • status: (string)

      Status of the measurement.

    • compartment: required (string)

      The compartment where the sample was taken from.

    • measurementdate: required (datetime-only)

      Date/time of the measurement.

    • quantity: required (string)

      The quantity the measured value is expressed in.

    • parametertype: (union of string or nil)

      Type of parameter measured.

    • parametergroup: (union of string or nil)

      The parameter group used for measuring.

    • taxontype: (union of string or nil)

      The type of taxon if the parameter was a taxon.

    • parameter: (string)

      The code of the parameter measured.

    • note: (union of string or nil)

      Specification of the measurement.

    • limitsymbol: (union of string or nil)

      Limit symbol as a specification of the measured value.

    • measuredvalue: (number)

      The value measured.

    • measuredunit: required (string)

      The unit of the measured value.

    • calculatedvalue: (union of number or nil)

      The calculated value (mostly micro-biology).

    • calculatedunit: (union of string or nil)

      The unit of the calculated value.

    • classifiedvalue: (union of string or nil)

      Classification of the measurement.

    • projects: (array of string)

      Projects for which the measurement took place.

    • measurementattributes: (array of string)

      Qualification of what was measured, i.e. gender, life form.

    • collectiondate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

      The date the measurement took place.

    • changedate: (union of datetime-only or nil)

      Measurement change date.

    • taxongroup: (union of string or nil)

      Taxon group.

    • measurementsetnumber: (union of string or nil)

      Measurement set number.

    • measurementsetattributes: (array of string)

      Measurement set attributes.

Example:

{
    "totalObjectCount": 376494,
    "links": {
        "self": "/eco/measurements?page=1&pagesize=3",
        "prev": null,
        "next": "/eco/measurements?page=2&pagesize=3",
        "maxPageSize": 10000,
        "defaultPageSize": 1000,
        "minPageSize": 1
    },
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1",
        "responseType": "MeasurementsListResponse"
    },
    "result": [
        {
            "calculatedunit": "N/ML",

        }
    ]
}

HTTP status code 400

Body

Media type: application/json

Type: object

Properties
  • provider: required (object)

    Information regarding the system that is responible for the response. Provides support contact information in case there are issues with response format or content.

    • name: (string)
    • supportUrl: required (string)
    • apiVersion: (string)
    • responseType: (string)
  • type: required (string)

    Error type.

  • typeinfo: (union of string or nil)

    Link to information on the type of error.

  • status: required (integer)

    HTTP status code.

  • title: required (string)

    Title of the error.

  • detail: required (string)

    Details of the error.

  • instance: (union of string or nil)

    Unique identification of the error for analysis.

  • errors: (array of Minimal.FilterError)

    Error details.

    Items: FilterError

    • errortype: required (string)
    • context: required (string)

Example:

{
    "type": "Filter query syntax",
    "typeinfo": null,
    "title": "Query syntax",
    "status": 400,
    "detail": "See 'errors' attribute.",
    "instance": null,
    "provider": {
        "name": "EcoSys",
        "supportUrl": "www.ecosys.nl",
        "apiVersion": "0.9.1"
    },
    "errors": [
        {
            "errortype": "InvalidSyntax",
            "context": "unsupportedfiltertest"
        }
    ]
}

/eco/measurements/geojson get

Retrieves a list of measurements as a GeoJSON FeatureCollection.

get

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

get /eco/measurements/geojson

Defines query parameters for pageable requests.

  • Request
  • Response

Query Parameters

  • page: (integer)

    Page number, starting with 1.

  • pagesize: (integer)

    Page size. Minimum, maximum and default is defined by provider. Minimum can never be lower than 1.

  • filter: (string)

    Filter the data, based on the filter. See Search syntax.

Type: array of object

    Filter comparer.

    Filter data type.
